. ///     LOAD DATA
> use data/csrhub-kld-cstat-year-level-with-treatment-variables.dta, clear

. 
. est clear

. 
. /// SET PANEL
> encode cusip, gen(cusip_n)

. xtset cusip_n year, y
       panel variable:  cusip_n (unbalanced)
        time variable:  year, 1990 to 2018, but with gaps
                delta:  1 year

. 
. ///     GENERATE YEAR-ON-YEAR REVENUE CHANGE
> gen revt_yoy = revt - l.revt
(74,693 missing values generated)

. label var revt_yoy "Year-on-year change in revenue (revt)"

. 
. ///     KEEP VARIABLES IN REGRESSION MODELS TO REDUCE FILE SIZE
> keep cusip cusip_n year revt revt_yoy dltt at xad xrd emp age ///
>         over_rtg *rtg_lym sic tobinq

. 
.         
.                                                 ***===========================***
.                                                 *       FIXED EFFECTS REGRESSION        *

. ***===========================***
. *       REVENUE LEVEL = F (CSRHUB)      *
. ***===========================***
. ///     CONTROL VARIABLE MODELS
> 
. ***     DV: Revenue (Level)
. *mark mark3
. *markout mark3 revt over_rtg dltt at xad xrd emp year
. 
. qui xtreg revt over_rtg, fe cluster(cusip_n)                                                                            

. est store revtmod1

. estadd local yearFE "No", replace

added macro:
             e(yearFE) : "No"

. qui xtreg revt over_rtg i.year, fe cluster(cusip_n)

. *       REVENUE CHANGE = F (CSRHUB)     *
. ***===============================***   
. /// DV: Revenue (1-year change)
> local dv revt_yoy

. local iv over_rtg 

. local controls "dltt at age emp tobinq xad xrd"

. 
. qui xtreg revt `iv', fe cluster(cusip_n)

. est store over_rtgmod0

. estadd local yearFE "No", replace

added macro:
             e(yearFE) : "No"

. 
. qui xtreg revt `iv' i.year, fe cluster(cusip_n)

. est store over_rtgmod1

. estadd local yearFE "Yes", replace

added macro:
             e(yearFE) : "Yes"

. 
. local vars ""

. local counter 2

. foreach control of local controls {
  2.         *       Regression
.         qui xtreg revt `iv' `vars' `control' i.year, fe cluster(cusip_n)
  3.                 
.         *       Store results
.         est store over_rtgmod`counter'
  4.         estadd local yearFE "Yes", replace
  5.         
.         *       Increment
.         local vars "`vars' `control'"
  6.         local counter = `counter' + 1
  7. }

added macro:
             e(yearFE) : "Yes"

             e(yearFE) : "Yes"

. 
. *       Assume missing xad and xrd are 0, interact over_rtg and revt, 
. *       all independent variables lagged
. preserve

(43,211 real changes made)

. replace xrd=0 if xrd==. & over_rtg!=.                                                                                   /*      assumption      */
(41,111 real changes made)

. 
. qui xtreg revt c.over_rtg##c.revt dltt at age emp tobinq xad xrd i.year, fe cluster(cusip_n)

. est store over_rtgint1

. estadd local yearFE "Yes", replace

added macro:
             e(yearFE) : "Yes"

. restore

. 
. *       Assume missing xad and xrd are 0, interact over_rtg and revt, 
. *       all independent variables lagged, and standardized revt and over_rtg
. preserve

. replace xad=0 if xad==. & over_rtg!=.                                                                                   /*      assumption      */
(43,211 real changes made)

. replace xrd=0 if xrd==. & over_rtg!=.                                                                                   /*      assumption      */
(41,111 real changes made)

. 
. egen Sover_rtg = std(over_rtg)
(126629 missing values generated)

. egen Srevt = std(revt)
(67607 missing values generated)

. 
. qui xtreg revt c.Sover_rtg##c.Srevt dltt at emp tobinq xad xrd age i.year, fe cluster(cusip_n)

. est store over_rtgint2

. estadd local yearFE "Yes", replace

added macro:
             e(yearFE) : "Yes"

. restore

> tg_lym board_rtg_lym ldrship_ethics_rtg_lym trans_report_rtg_lym"

. local controls "dltt at age emp tobinq xad xrd"

. foreach iv of local ivs {
  2.         local vars ""
  3.         display "`iv'"
  4.         xtreg revt `iv', fe cluster(cusip_n)
  5.         est store `iv'0
  6.         qui estadd local yearFE "No", replace
  7.         qui estadd local firmFE "Yes", replace
  8. 
.         xtreg revt `iv' i.year, fe cluster(cusip_n)
  9.         est store `iv'1
 10.         qui estadd local yearFE "Yes", replace
 11.         qui estadd local firmFE "Yes", replace
 12.         
.         local vars ""
 13.         local counter 2
 14.         foreach control of local controls {
 15.                 *       Regression
.                 xtreg revt `iv' `vars' `control' i.year, fe cluster(cusip_n)
 16.                         
.                 *       Store results
.                 est store `iv'`counter'
 17.                 estadd local yearFE "Yes", replace
 18.                 estadd local firmFE "Yes", replace
 19.                 
.                 *       Increment
.                 local vars "`vars' `control'"
 20.                 local counter = `counter' + 1
 21.         }
 22. 
.         esttab `iv'*, ///
>                 keep(`iv' dltt at age emp tobinq xad xrd) ///
>                 order(`iv' dltt at age emp tobinq xad xrd) ///
>                 s(yearFE firmFE N N_g r2 aic, label("Year FEs" "Firm FEs" "Observations" "Firms" "R^2" "AIC"))
 23. 
.         *       Many xad and xrd observations are missing. Assume missing = 0.
.         preserve
 24.         replace xad=0 if xad==. & `iv'!=.                                                                                       /*      assumption      */
 25.         replace xrd=0 if xrd==. & `iv'!=.                                                                                       /*      assumption      */
 26. 
.         xtreg revt `iv' `controls' i.year, fe cluster(cusip_n)
 27.         est store as1
 28.         qui estadd local yearFE "Yes", replace
 29.         qui estadd local firmFE "Yes", replace
 30.         restore 
 31. 
.         *       Table
.         esttab `iv'* as1, ///
>                 keep(`iv' dltt at age emp tobinq xad xrd) ///
>                 order(`iv' dltt at age emp tobinq xad xrd) ///
>                 s(yearFE firmFE N N_g r2 aic, label("Year FEs" "Firm FEs" "Observations" "Firms" "R^2" "AIC"))
 32. }
